chauthi gend par unhone ek ran liya or strike braavo ko thamaya

 antim gend par match jeetne ke liye superkings ko paanch ran banane the or bhaatia kii antim gend par braavo ne chakka jadkar apni team ko jeet dilaa di
 Dhoni scored 28 runs for a total of 151 and was dismissed on the second ball of the 20th over
 dhoni ne 21 gendon kaa saamana kiya or teen chauke or ek chakka lagaaya
 Bravo returned unbeaten pavilion after scoring 11 runs off seven balls while Jadeja returned unbeaten after scoring three runs from two balls
 niterides kii ore se bhaatia or narin ne do-do wicket hasil kiye
 Earlier, the Kolkata Knight Riders captain led by Gautam Gambhir scored 158 for the loss of six wickets in the stipulated 20 overs, batting first after losing the toss
 niterides kii ore se gautam gambheer ne 62 or brendan maiklam ne 37 ranon kaa yogadan diya
 Knight Riders openers Gambhir and mccallum gave a 99-run partnership, giving their team a solid start
 niterides kaa pehla wicket 12wein over main maiklam ke rup main gira
 mccullum scored 37 runs in 29 balls with the help of four fours and a six
 gautam gambhir 62 ran ke nijee yoga par 13wein over main jakaati kii gend par bold ho gaye
 He hit six fours and three sixes in 43 balls
 iske baad jacks kallis chaar, yusuf pathan 11 or manoj tiwari 12 or lakshmiratan shukla nau ran banaakar saste main out ho gaye
 Devbrata Das 19 and Rajat Bhatia remained unbeaten after scoring one run
 superkings kii ore se shaadaab jakaati ko do wicket mili jabaki ben hilphenhas, ravichandran aswin or rabindra jadeja ko ek-ek safalataa mili
 The comments niterides ne ab tak 13 match khele hai jinamein se use aath main jeet jabaki chaar maichon main haar mili he

 17 ank lekar niterides talika main tisare sthaan par he
 If the Knight Riders win the match, they will be on 19 points and will overtake the top-ranked Delhi Daredevils (18) to finish in first place

 One match was inconclusive due to rain
 15 ank lekar superkings talika main chauthe sthaan par he
 The win puts the Superkings on 17 points
 haar ke baavjood niterides ke bhi 17 hi ank he lekin behatar ran rate ke aadhaar par vah tisare or superkings chauthe sthaan par he
 The Chennai Super Kings team achieved the target of 159 runs laid by Kolkata Knight Riders team on the last ball
 antim gend par chennai ko jeet ke liye paanch ranon kii darkaar thi or dwen braavo ne chakka jadkar apni team ko jeet dilaa di
 Hussey and Vijay opened the innings for the Superkings and both added 97 runs in 62 balls for the first wicket
 isi yoga par hasi ke rup main superkings ko pehla jhatka laga
 Hussey smashed 56 off 39 balls
 apni is pari ke dauraan unhone chaar chauke or chaar chakke lagaae
 Hussey was declared man of the match for his innings
 do gendon ke baad isi yoga par vijay bhi chalate bane
 He scored 36 off 25 balls
 vijay ne paanch chauke or ek chakka lagaaya
 Hussey and Vijay took wickets by Sunil Narine
 110 ke yoga par suraish raina ke ran out ho jane se laga ki superkings kii team mushkilon main pad sakati he
 He could only score eight runs
 superkings kii mushkilen tab or bad gai jab 127 ke kul yoga par phalf du plasis bhi out ho gaye
 He scored 13 runs and was dismissed by Rajat Bhatia
 antim over main superkings ko jeetne ke liye nau ran banane the or krij par the captain mahendra singh dhoni or braavo
 On the first ball, Bravo took a run and gave the batting to Dhoni, but Dhoni was bowled on the second ball
 iske baad ballebaaji karne aae rabindra jadeja ne teesri gend par do ran liye
 On the fourth ball, he took a run and gave the strike to Bravo
 braavo paanchavi gend miss kar gaye or phir match main aayaa jabardast romaanch
 The Superkings had to score five runs to win the match on the final ball, and on Bhatia's last ball, Bravo hit his team to a six
 151 ke kul yoga par dhoni 28 ran banaakar 20wein over kii duusari gend par out hue
 Dhoni faced 21 balls and hit three fours and a six
 braavo saat gendon par 11 ran banaakar naabad pavilion laute vahiin jadeja do gendon par teen ran banaakar naabad laute
 For the Knight Riders, Bhatia and Narine took two wickets each
 isse pehle, gautam gambheer kii captaini vaali kolkata niterides team ne toss haarane ke baad pehle ballebaaji karte hue nirdhaarit 20 over main chah wicket ke nuksaan par 158 ran banaae
 For the Knight Riders, Gautam Gambhir contributed 62 and Brendon mccullum contributed 37 runs
 niterides ke salaami ballebaaj gambheer or maiklam ne apni team ko thos shuruyaat dete hue 99 ranon kii saajhedaari kii
 The Knight Riders' first wicket fell in the 12th over as mccallum
 maiklam ne 29 gendo main chaar chauke or ek chakke kii madad se 37 ran banaakar ranout hue
 Gautam Gambhir was bowled by Jakati in the 13th over on a personal total of 62 runs
 unhone 43 gendon main chah chauke or teen chakke lagaae
 After this Jacques Kallis was dismissed cheaply by four, Yusuf Pathan 11 and Manoj Tiwari 12 and Laxmiratan Shukla nine
 devabrata das 19 or rajat bhaatia ek ran banaakar naabad rahe
 From the Superkings, Shadab Jakati got two wickets, while Ben Hilfenhaus, Ravichandran Ashwin and Ravindra Jadeja had one success each
 tippaniyan The Knight Riders have played 13 matches so far, of which they have won eight and lost four
 ek muqabla barish ke kaaran radd ho gaya tha
 Knightriders are third in the table with 17 points
 yadi niterides is mukaable ko jeet jaati he to uske 19 ank ho jaaenge or vah sheersh par chal rahi dilli dairedevills (18) ko apdasth kar pehle sthaan par pahunch jaaegi
 The Superkings have played 14 matches so far, of which they have won seven and lost six matches
 ek muqabla barish ke kaaran benatija rahaa tha
 The Superkings are fourth in the table with 15 points
 kolkata niterides team kii ore se rakhe gaye 159 ranon ke lakshya ko chennai superkings team ne antim gend par hasil kiya
 Chennai needed five runs to win on the final ball and Dwayne Bravo hit a six to give his team the victory

 hasi ko unki is pari ke liye main of da match ghoshit kiya gaya

 nyaayamurti manmohan ne kaha ki kripaya apane gharon (khel sanghon) main sudhaar kar lo

 khel nikaayon main ab koi vishwaas nahin rah gaya he

 adaalat bhartiya kushti mahasang (dablyooefai), punjab kushti sangh or chhattisgarh kushti sangh se judi yachika par sunwaayee kar rahi thi
 The court said that it cannot be that persons who have never played sports should hold the posts of sports bodies
 aise nikaayon main kam se kam ek aisa vyakti adhyaksh or upaadhyaksh hona chahie jisane rajya str par khel khelaa ho

 input: IANS a North Korean diplomat said in Geneva that the nuclear test conducted by his country on February 12 was a measure of self-defense in response to ever-increasing threats from the US

 In response to the responses from the US, John said that if the US adopts a hostile attitude towards North Korea, it will only make the situation more complicated and force North Korea to take more stringent measures
 tippaniyan According to media reports, North Korea also threatened the final destruction of South Korea at the conference
 america ne kaha he ki parmaanu pareekshan kisi bhi tarah se surakshatmak kadam nahin he
 North Korea has violated international obligations and UN resolutions, according to which North Korea cannot conduct further nuclear tests
